People sometimes say I'm exaggerating when I say 99% of Kyokushin Jin's playerbase "barely scratch the character's surface". Due to him being the most extreme character in the game in terms of reflex-based plays, by having an arsenal of perfectly tailored answers/punishers to basically every defensive situation in the game (answers that must be found hidden within his movelist/given immediately in order to actually work) and by being virtually the ultimate character, specially in a controlled environment (IE Tool-Assisted videos). He can perfectly answer questions no other character can, and I could give some examples if someone asked.  Then I play around with stuff like these and realize they are wrong and I am really not exaggerating: there's no skill ceiling to this character. The sky is the limit and most players barely reach for it. This character is the coolest elitist thing ever, and it's a pride and joy to main him. :)
